import re


def main():
    rawData = []
    with open('h1.txt', 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        rawData = f.readlines()
    # print(len(rawData))

    # pattern = re.compile('(\d+)%29%29%3E(\d+)   idï¼š(1)?<br><br>')
    pattern = re.compile('(\d{1,2})1%29%29%3E(\d+)\s+idï¼š(\d)?<br><br>')

    strLen = 0
    resultDict = {}
    for each in range(250):
        m = pattern.search(rawData[1+each*6])
        # print(m.group(1))
        # print(m.group(2))
        # print(m.group(3))
        m1 = int(m.group(1))
        m2 = int(m.group(2))
        m3 = 0
        if m.group(3) != None:
            m3 = 1
        # print(m3)
        if  m1 > strLen:
            strLen = m1
        
        if resultDict.get(m1):
            if m3 == 1:
                if m2 > resultDict[m1]['s']:
                    resultDict[m1]['s'] = m2
            else:
                if m2 < resultDict[m1]['b']:
                    resultDict[m1]['b'] = m2
                    
        else:                    
            if m3 == 1:
                tempDict = {
                    'character': m1,
                    's': m2,
                    'b': 1000,
                }
            else:
                tempDict = {
                    'character': m1,
                    's': 0,
                    'b': m2,
                }
                resultDict[m1] = tempDict
    # print(strLen) # é•¿åº¦ä¸º20
    for each in range(strLen):
        print(chr(resultDict[each+1]['b']), end='')



if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
